
1a1(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul dra ba le'u stong phrag brgya pa las rtsa ba'i rgyud dpal gsang ba snying po'i don bsdus 'brel paN+DA rtha bzhugs/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di t+ta chen po bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa'o//
1b1(rgyud 'grel): bcom ldan 'das dpal kun tu bzang po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /mnyam nyid dbyings su bdud bzhi dang
1b2(rgyud 'grel): gis bcom/ /phyag rgya'i rang bzhin gnyis med rdzogs par ldan/ /yod med mdza' 'das bdag gzhan yongs kyi dpal/ /
1b3(rgyud 'grel): thams cad rang bzhin rtogs dang thugs rje bzang/ /kun bzang lha'i lha khyod dbyer med la/ /rtogs dang grub pas rab tu
1b4(rgyud 'grel): phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang zhig sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud 'di nyid/ /don rtogs gsal bar bya phyir bdag gis ni/ /don
2a1(rgyud 'grel): bsdus rab tu dbye ba 'di brtsams pas/ /dngos grub mchog gnyis thob par bya phyir bshad/ /gang gis rgyud
2a2(rgyud 'grel): 'di rtogs dka' bas/ /bde rlag du ni rtogs par 'gyur/ /'di yi rang bzhin che ba dang/ /mtshan nyid dang ni don bstan phyir/ /
2a3(rgyud 'grel): sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud chen las/ /mdor bsdus bstan la phab pa yin/ /rang bzhin gsang bzhes bya ste/ /che ba zhes ni snying po'i
2a4(rgyud 'grel): don/ /de kho na nyid mtshan nyid do/ /nges pas nges don mdor bstan pa/ /de ltar rnam pa bzhi po ru/ /mdor bsdus spyi'i don
2b1(rgyud 'grel): du bshad/ /rang bzhin gab dang rbas pa dang/ /bstan min zhes bya'i rang bzhin ni/ /mnyam pa nyid dang dgongs pa'i don/ /mdzad spyod gsang ba'i theg
2b2(rgyud 'grel): pa nyid/ /rnam bzhi gsang ba zhes pa'i mtshan/ /sde snod rgyud kun 'byung phyir dang/ /bstan la 'bebs dang khyad par che/ /ston pa 'khor dang gnas
2b3(rgyud 'grel): las sogs/ /mchog tu gyur pas che ba bshad/ /rgyu dang 'bras bu dbyer med pa/ /don dam kun rdzob gnyis med ni/ /mtshan nyid zhes bya rnam pa
2b4(rgyud 'grel): gsum/ /lung dang man ngag nges pa yang/ /nges pa'i dbyings nas phyung bas na/ /nges don don ni bstan pa yin/ /nges don spyi'i mtshan nyid ni/ /so so rnam
2b5(rgyud 'grel): grangs don rnams kyi/ /sngon du 'gro ba'i bdag nyid pas/ /ming nyid thog mar smos pa gces/ /rgyu dang rkyen dang gzhung nyid dang/ /'gro ba'i don du
3a1(rgyud 'grel): snang ba'i phyir/ /gleng gzhi dang ni gleng slangs te/ /don dang yongs su gzung ba dang/ /rnam pa bzhi ni bsdus pa yin/ /gleng gzhi rnam pa
3a2(rgyud 'grel): ldar bshad de/ /gang tshe gang gi gang du bshad/ /gang la gang gis bsdus pa ste/ /'byung ba dus dang ston pa dang/ /gnas dang 'khor dang sdud pa'o/ /sgro
3a3(rgyud 'grel): dang skur bzhi bas na/ /'di skad zhes su bshad pa yin/ /sku gsung thugs kyis bshad pas na/ /ma rtogs skyon dang gsung thos skyon/ /bshad ces
3a4(rgyud 'grel): pas ni spangs pa yin/ /bla med 'khor lo bskor ba'i tshe/ /de tshe dus zhes bya bar grags/ /ston pa zhes bya'i mtshan nyid ni/ /rang bzhin dang ni mdzad
3a5(rgyud 'grel): spyod dang/ /rnal 'byor rnam gnyis ngo la snang/ /byang chub chen po'i rang bzhin dang/ /chos rnams rol par longs spyod dang/ /phyogs dus bde
3b1(rgyud 'grel): gshegs bdag po dang/ /chos so cig dang dbyer med pa/ /ston pa'i rang bzhin rnam pa bzhi/ /don dam chos kyi sku'i mtshan/ /mdzad spyod gzugs sku rnam gnyis te/ /longs spyod rdzogs dang sprul sku'o/ /longs
3b2(rgyud 'grel): spyod sngags kyi bdag po'i tshul/ /rgyal po rgyal mo yang dag ldan/ /sprul pa rdul snyed thub pa dang/ /khro rgyal stsogs pa grangs med yin/ /bdag po sku'i mtshan nyid dang/ /zhal dang mtshan? dang dpe byad
3b3(rgyud 'grel): dang/ /bsam 'das zhabs dang phyag mtshan dang/ /dbu dang sku dang kha dog dang/ /rgyal mo'i tshogs dang bzhugs pa'i dpe/ /bcu dang gsum gyis rdzogs par rol/ /ye shes phyi nang med pa dang/ /thams
3b4(rgyud 'grel): cad mnyam par dgongs pa dang/ /sems dpa' sems mar ldan pa dang/ /bcu drug rgyas btab dpe byad dang/ /lus dang ngag sems cis 'dus par/ /de rnyed sku gsung snang ba dang/ /thabs dang shes rab snang
3b5(rgyud 'grel): ba dang/ /ye shes drug dang phyag rgya drug /rnam thar sku gsum bsam yas dang/ /phung po lnga po'i ngo bo nyid/ /rgyal ba lnga ru rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /kun kyang kha dog lnga pa ste/ /nyi shu rtsa lnga rin chen mdog/
3b6(rgyud 'grel): snang bar mnyen dro bskyod dang lnga/ /dbyings kyi ngo bo rgyal mo ste/ /de bzhin kro te rnam lnga min/ /nam mkha' dbyings kyi mdza' klas pa/ /ston pa'i mdzad spyod rol mo yis/ /til gyi gang bu bzhin du khyab/ /
4a1(rgyud 'grel): ston pa'i khyad par yin par grags/ /gnas ni rnam pa gsum du grags/ /chos kyi dbyings dang gzhal yas khang/ /bag chos 'byung zhes su bya/ /mdza' dbus med pa chos kyi
4a2(rgyud 'grel): dbyings/ /de ni gnas kyi bla mar 'dod/ /gzhal yas gzhi dang rgyu dang rgya/ /dbyibs dang blo 'bur rtse mo dang/ /rgyan dang sgo khyud rta babs dang/ /mtshan nyid gdan gyi rnam pa ste/ /bcu gcig
4a3(rgyud 'grel): dag gis rnam par dbye'o/ /gzhi'i yang tshad med 'khor lo ste/ /ye shes lnga yi rang bzhin yin/ /ye shes phyogs bzhi dbus brtags pas/ /rin chen las byas gzhal yas khang/ /che chung yo
4a4(rgyud 'grel): bu ma byas pa/ /chos dbyings mdza' la khyab par snang/ /rgyas par rgyas phyir gru bzhi pa'o/ /kun las spags pa'i gzungs bzhi dang/ /ye shes bzhi'i ngo bo nyid/ /gcig la'ang ye shes kun gnas
4a5(rgyud 'grel): dang/ /gzhal byas mdzes par byas pa'i phyir/ /glo 'bur bzhi yang mkhar thabs tshul/ /bum pa'i rtse mo chos kyi rtog /chos kyi dbyings su kun nas gnas/ /glo 'bur lnga'i brgyan rnams kyang/ /dbyingS
4a6(rgyud 'grel): dang kha dog bye drag dag /rigs kyi khyad par gyis ni dbye/ /gnas mchog nyid kyi rgyan mchog kyang/ /gzugs sgra dri ro reg gi rnams/ /rigs kyi khyad par gyis ni brtag /so sor ma bsgrib dang
4b1(rgyud 'grel): gis gsal/ /bar chad med par phyogs bcur 'khrigs/ /stong smon mtshan med 'od gsal 'jug /de phyir ye shes sgo khyud can/ /nyan thos rang rgyal byang chub dang/ /
4b2(rgyud 'grel): bya ba rgyud dang gnyi ga rgyud/ /rnal 'byor skyed dang rdzogs pa yi/ /rnam thar brgyad phyir rta babs brgyad/ /gnas mchog mtshan nyid brjod pa ni/ /gzhal yas phyi dang
4b3(rgyud 'grel): chos dbyings nang/ /bdag nyid du ni bsdus pas na/ /kun tu nang zhes bshad pa yin/ /de na gnas pa'i gdan mchog kyang/ /seng ge glang chen rta dang khyung/ /nam mkha' 
4b4(rgyud 'grel): lding gi khri chen la/ /nyi zla pad+ma rin po che/ /lnga rtsegs nyi shu rtsa lngar ldan/ /rgyal po rgyal mo'i gdan mchog la/ /mi 'jigs bzhi dang stobs bcu dang/ /rdzu
4b5(rgyud 'grel): 'phrul bzhi dang dbang rnams bcu/ /thogs med 'phrin las rnam bzhi'o/ /thabs dang shes rab 'od gsal 'bar/ /skyon gyi sa ma gos zad mi shes/ /
4b6(rgyud 'grel): sngon sangs rgyas dang zag pa zad/ /bar mi chod dang nges par 'byung/ /'jig rten 'jig rten 'das bcas la/ /'jigs med pa'i sems kyis su/ /
5a1(rgyud 'grel): chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor/ /gnas dang gnas min yang dag mkhyen/ /dus gsum las 'das rnam smin mkhyen/ /khams rnams sna tshogs mkhyen pa dang/ /pha rol mos pa mkhyen pa'i
5a2(rgyud 'grel): stobs/ /dbang po mchog dang mchog min mkhyen/ /kun tu 'gro lam mkhyen pa'i stobs/ /bsam gtan thar dang nyon mongs mkhyen/ /sngon gyi gnas mkhyen stobs dang ni/ /skye dang 'chi 'pho mkhyen pa dang/ /zag pa zag med sems grol mkhyen/ /de bcu stobs
5a3(rgyud 'grel): bcur gyur pas na/ /'bras bu sngon shes drug yin no/ /'dun dang brtson 'grus sems dang ni/ /spyod pa'i ting 'dzin spong ba yin/ /'du byed rnams te rkang pa bzhi/ /ye shes bzhi grub 'bras bu ste/ /chos dbyings ye shes kun la khyab/ /yo byad skye ba
5a4(rgyud 'grel): tshe la dbang/ /ye shes chos dang sems dang las/ /rdzu 'phrul smon lam mos rnams kyi/ /khams kun gyis ni dbang phyug rgyal/ /zhi rgyas dbang drag las rnams kyis/ /thog med las rnams lhun gyis grub/ /ci la thogs pa med par spyod//
5a5(rgyud 'grel): gnas mchog khyad par de nyid kyang/ /dbyings phyug ba gar bstan pa yin/ /'khor rnams bkod pa ji snyed pa/ /khams dang skye mched yin par grags/ /rnam shes yul dang dbang po dang/ /dus dang phyin ci ma log rnams/ /byang chub chen po'i
5a6(rgyud 'grel): rang bzhin du/ /lhun gyis grub pa'i dkyil 'khor yin/ /mthong dang thos dang snoms dang myong/ /rnam shes bzhi po sems dpar shar/ /mthong bya thos bya snoms bya dang/ /myong bya 'dod pa'i lha mo rnams/ /rnam shes bzhi dang dbyer med par//
5a7(rgyud 'grel): mdzes? pa'i blo 'bur bzhi po la/ /nyi zla pad+ma rin chen gdan/ /mthong byed thos byed snoms byed dang/ /myong byed dbang po'i sems dpa' dang/ /'das dang da ltar byung 'od dang/ /'byung bar ma nges lha mo bzhi/ /dbyer med tshul du grwa bzhir gnas/ /reg pa reg
5b1(rgyud 'grel): byed reg bya dang/ /yid kyi khams te 'joms byed dang/ /rtag chad bdag tu ma yin dang/ /mtshan ma ma yin 'joms pa rnams/ /sgo bzhi phyogs su de bzhin gnas/ /kun bzang yid kyi rnam shes dang/ /chos ni bya ba kun tu bzang/ /mdun dang rgyab tu rnam par gnas/ /de nyid
5b2(rgyud 'grel): bsdud pa phun sum tshogs/ /bsdu bya'i yul ni chos yin te/ /byed pa po ni kun tu bzang/ /thugs kyi thugs te thugs yin no/ /srid gsum 'gro ba thams cad kyis/ /phung po khams dang skye mched dag/ brjod med brjod kyis mi langs pa/ /de snyed 'khor lo dkyil
5b3(rgyud 'grel): 'khor du/ /sngon rdzogs rgyal po de nyid nges/ /gnyis med lhun grub dkyil 'khor na/ /thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu bzhugs/ /de nas ston pa bde gshegs rnams/ /btsun mo'i tshogs dang gnyis med pa'i/ /gsang ba mchog gi dkyil 'khor rnams/ /rgyud 'di
5b4(rgyud 'grel): nyid kyi mdo don ste/ /dkyil 'khor kun gyi gsang ba 'di/ /sku gsung yon tan 'phrin las thugs/ /rdo rje las ni nges par byung/ /ngo mtshar dkyil 'khor brjod pa'i tshig /e zhes bya ba ngam pa'i don/ /e ma zhes bya rab tu dam/ /e ma ho zhes bya shin tu ngam/ /dkyil
5b5(rgyud 'grel): 'khor rnam pa bcu gnyis te/ /de bzhin nyid dang rang bzhin dang/ /thugs rjes 'dul ba'i dkyil 'khor dang/ /ting nge 'dzin dang gzugs brnyan dang/ /lhag pa'i ting 'dzin gzugs brnyan dang/ /byang chub sems dang lhag byang sems/ /tshogs dang lhun grub dkyil
5b6(rgyud 'grel): 'khor ro/ /chos kyi dbyings nyid de bzhin nyid/ /ye shes kyis ni dbang sgyur ba/ /rang bzhin thabs kyis dkyil 'khor nyid/ /thugs rje 'byung ba thugs rje'o/ /de nyid thugs rjes 'dul ba'i dang/ /rang snang dbyer med dkyil 'khor du/ /ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam par bsgom//
5b7(rgyud 'grel): rten 'byug? mtshon par byed pas na/ /gzugs brnyan sgyu ma'i dkyil 'khor ni/ /sgyu ma yin zhes rgyal bas gsungs/ /mkha' dbyings gsal bar rnams spyang pas/ /de yang rang snang zhes su bshad/ /sku gsung yon tan 'phrin las thugs/ /de nyid mtshon pa'i
6a1(rgyud 'grel): thabs tshul du/ /sa la sogs la phyag rgya byas/ /lhag pa'i gzugs brnyan yin par grags/ /dam pa'i don gyi byang chub sems/ /til 'bru bzhin ni kun la khyab/ /a'i bo de rab tu bsdus/ /byang chub rdo rje dri las byung/ /lhag pa yid
6a2(rgyud 'grel): bzhin rin po che/ /sku gsung thugs ni mi zad pa/ /gter ldan brgyan gyi 'khor lo nyid/ /tshogs chen rdzogs pa ces su bshad/ /chos sku rdo rje mchog nyid do/ /ma bcos lhun grub bdag nyid do/ /mnyam nyid dbyings kyi de bzhin nyid/ /man zhes bya ba snying
6a3(rgyud 'grel): po'i don/ /de la zhes bya len pa'o/ /yul dang dbang po yin par dgongs/ /spyod yul kun tu maN+Dal/ /rdo rje gsang bas gsung ba dang/ /brjod dka' de nyid brjod pas na/ /rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig du'o/ /brjod du med pa'i ngo bo nyid/ /tshig tu brjod pa ma yin yang/ /
6a4(rgyud 'grel): 'dzub mo sgron ma zla ba gser/ /don mtshon tshig ni don dang 'dra/ /don ni mi rtogs med min pa'o/ /dbul po'i gter dang gyad nor 'dra/ /tshig ni me long sgron me'i tshul/ /'gro ba'i don la brjod par bshad/ /des na bde gshegs rgyal ba rnams/ /nyid la nyid
6a5(rgyud 'grel): kyis gsung mod kyi/ /'gro la phan pa'i don gyi phyir/ /brjod pa nyid du rgyal bas gsung/ /gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o// //de nas ston pa rgyal mchog gis/ /dkyil 'khor mdo'i don gleng ba/ /de nyid don 'di bsdus 'dod nas/ /yab yum
6a6(rgyud 'grel): gnyis po gleng ba yin/ /yab kyi ye shes don glengs pa/ /gang gis ji ltar gang glengs dang/ /glengs pa'i 'bras bu nyid dang bzhi/ /thams cad kun gyi byed pa po/ /kun bzang yid nyid rdo rje te/ /ye shes rdo rje 'dus pa'i tshul/ /rang rig dbyings la 'jug
6a7(rgyud 'grel): 'gyur te/ /srid dang rnam grol thams cad kun/ /thig le'i tshul du dbyer med pas/ /ston pa rdo rje bde gshegs la/ /kun bzang bde bar gshegs nyid kyis/ /'gro ba'i mched du 'di skad brjod/ /rang gi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor la/ /ngo mtshar gyis ni?
6b1(rgyud 'grel): tshig brjod de/ /srid dang rnam grol thams cad kyi/ /phung po'i yan lag rnam pa lnga/ /chos sku rdo rje yin pa'i phyir/ /rgyal po lnga ru rnam par grags/ /'gro ba'i 'gro ba thams cad kyi/ /khams dang skye mched rnam pa kun/ /sems pa sems ma'i dkyil 'khor yin/ /khamS
6b2(rgyud 'grel): lnga dbyings phyug rgyal mo lnga/ /mdor na srid gsum thams cad kun/ /mngon rdzogs rgyal por de nyid nges/ /'di skad chig tu gleng ba'i cho/ /rgyal ba rigs lnga'i dkyil 'khor rnams/ /'gro ba'i ched du mnyes gyur nas/ /yum gyi dbyings kyi don glengs pa/ /gang
6b3(rgyud 'grel): gis ji ltar ji skad glengs/ /glengs pa'i 'bras bu nyid dang bzhi/ /bya ba mo ni kun tu bzang/ /ye shes la ni dbyings phyug 'gyur/ /'gro ba'i mched du gleng ba ni/ /stong gsum rdul snyed phyogs bcu kun/ /dngos por ma grub ye nas dbyen/ /srid gsum 'gro
6b4(rgyud 'grel): pa'i gnas nyid las/ /zhing khams dag las gud na med/ /nyon mongs dus tsho lta ba sems can nyid/ /snyigs ma lnga po 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal ste/ /bde chen gnas nyid las ni gzhan ma yin/ /nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po las/ /bde gshegs gud
6b5(rgyud 'grel): na yod ma yin/ /de bas thams cad snying po'i mchog /gzhan du sangs rgyas rtsal ma yin/ /de skad du tshig tu glengs pa'i tshe/ /bde chen dbyings su sangs rgyas par/ /ston pa rgyal mchog nyid kyis mkhyen/ /de nas rgyal po rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /btsun mo'i
6b6(rgyud 'grel): tshogs dang gnyis med pas/ /rnam gnyis glengs don thugs chung ste/ /gzhung don rnam pa bshad pa mdzad/ /rdzogs chen rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor pas/ /rtogs spyod rnam pa nyi shu yis/ /mngon rdzogs rgyal por de nyid nges/ /byang chub mchog tu
6b7(rgyud 'grel): sems bskyed pa/ /thog mar 'gro ba'i lam mchog yin/ /byang chub mchog ldan rnal 'byor nges/ /chos kun nges don gtan la phab/ /nges pa'i don nyid rtogs ba'i tsho/ /ming tsam snang ba'i chos rnams kun/ /yi ge 'khor lo mngon sangs rgyas//
7a1(rgyud 'grel): mngon rdzogs yi ge de nyid las/ /ting 'dzin rol mo mdza' yas 'phros/ /spros nyid dkyil 'khor bsam yas gsal/ /gsal byed sngags kyis yi ge brjod/ /de nyid thugs rtags phyag rgyar gsal/ /ma mthong smongs la
7a2(rgyud 'grel): bstan pa'i phyir/ /bkri dang rdul tshon bstan pa ces/ /dkyil 'khor dag la brten pa'i mi/ /dbang mchog sbyin pa mchog yin no/ /dbang mchog rdzogs nas tshogs la 'jug /tshogs bsgrub yon tan bsam mi khyab/ /tshogs mchog rgya cher
7a3(rgyud 'grel): spel ba yang/ /man ngag snying po can gyis bya/ /tshogs dus stong pa glu yis bya/ /gal te zhi bas mi 'dul na/ /rdo rje khro bo'i dkyil 'khor spro/ /khros pa'i sngags kyi bskur sten nas/ /dkyil 'khor nyid du bkod par bya/ /de nyid la ni mchod pa 'bul//
7a4(rgyud 'grel): zhi khro rab 'byam mchod pa'i tshe/ /sdom la gnas pa shin tu gces/ /dam tshig ldan pa'i skyes bu de/ /rnam bzhi las kyi gzhan don bya/ /khros pa'i glu'i bstod pa bya/ /don dam kun rdzob byang chub sems/ /rnam pa gnyis su ston pas gsung/ /rmad
7a5(rgyud 'grel): du byung ba'i byang chub sems/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba'i thugs/ /ye shes lnga'i rang bzhin ni/ /skye 'gag gnas dmigs 'gro 'ong rnams/ /don dam med las kun sgrib yod/ /don dam kun sgri dbyer med don/ /dam pa'i don du bde
7a6(rgyud 'grel): gshegs gsungs/ /brjod med de nyid brjod pa'i tshe/ /nyid kyi rtso bzungs 'khor lo mnyes/ /don ma rtogs dang snying rje dang/ /don mdzad kun rdzob rnam pa gsum/ /rgyal po rgyal mo 'khor bcas pas/ /rtogs dka' i gsang ba rnam bzhir brjod//
7a7(rgyud 'grel): di? nas rtogs dka' i gsang ba dang/ /sna tshogs chos rnams thams cad kyi/ /rang bzhin de nyid gsang ba dang/ /rang rang chos kyi ngo bo nyid/ /mtshan nyid so so rtogs pa gsang/ /snod min gzhan la mi bstan gsang/ /ma rtogs don nyid brjod pa yin/ /chos
7b1(rgyud 'grel): kun rang bzhin sangs rgyas kyang/ /de nyid ma rtogs 'khrul 'khor khyab/ /zhen pa bzlog phyir snying rje bskyed/ /rang bzhin gsang ba bstan pa'i phyir/ /chos sgo bsam yas spros pa mdzad/ /rang bzhin med pa'i chos nyid las/ /'gro ba 'khrul 'khor snang ba yang//?
7b2(rgyud 'grel): bdag 'dzin tsam las ma rtogs pa/ /'khrul 'khor dngos nyid ga la yong/ /dper na mkha' la mdud 'dor 'dra/ /bdag 'dzin 'ching ba dam po yang/ /bcings byed bcing bya ga la yod/ /de bas lhun grub dkyil 'khor che/ /de nyid bstan phyir bshad pa mdzad?//
7b3(rgyud 'grel): de skad bde gshegs rgyal mchog gis/ /'khor rnams bde gshegs dkyil 'khor la/ /'gro ba rnams kyi mched du gsung/ /sems bskyed pa'i le'u ste/ gnyis pa'o// //bstan la dbab par bya ba dang/ /bstan la phab ba gnyis su
7b4(rgyud 'grel): bshad/ /dbab bya sprul skus 'dul bstan la/ /nges pa'i don gyi bstan la phebs ces bya/ /gang las gang 'thon gang du ci byed dang/ /gang gis don mdzad yin te rnam pa lnga'o/ /gang las rgyal mchog sku gsung las/ /thugs rje rig pa'i thub
7b5(rgyud 'grel): drug mthon/ /gang du las kyi 'bras bu ste/ /stong gsum cig la chags tshul drug/ sprul sku cig gi zhing du grags/ /drug gi 'jig rten de nyid na/ /gling rnams bye ba phrag brgya yin/ /sprul pa bye ba phrag brgyar snang/ /gling rnams re rer sprul pa re re yang/ /'gro
7b6(rgyud 'grel): drug las kyi drug tu snang ba yin/ /dper na bar snang zla ba cig shar bas/ /'dzam bu gling gi chu rnams kun tu chu zlar snang/ /chu cig nang na snang ba'i zla ba yang/ /'gro ba so sos bltas na rang re'o? mdun na snang/ /de bzhin sprul sku cig la gling rnams snang/ /gling
7b7(rgyud 'grel): rnams cig las 'gro ba drug tu snang/ /tha dad de kun sprul pa cig tu grags de 'dra'i stong gsum mdza' yas mu med na/ /de 'dra'i sprul par res 'gro don de ltar mdzad/ /ci mdzad 'dul ba rnam pa bzhis/ /gang gis 'gro ba lnga don mdzad/ /mngon gsum rdzu
8a1(rgyud 'grel): 'phrul bsod nams rig pa bzhis/ /theg lnga'i rigs can 'gro lnga'i don rnams mdzad/ /mngon gsum 'dul bas sangs rgyas mdzad pa ston brdzu 'phrul mthun mong ma yin sngon shes drug/ bsod nams kun tu sku dang gsung thugs
8a2(rgyud 'grel): zhal/ /bsam gyis mi khyab grangs med phyogs bcur snang/ /rigs pas theg dang brgya bcur bzhir gsungs ba/ /'dul ba'i dbang gi theg lnga'i rigs dang sbyar/ /nyon mongs rnyen por sgo mang dus gsum gsungs/ /gzugs 'dzin phyi nang rten 'brel 'dul
8a3(rgyud 'grel): rnams la/ /mi dang lha dang nyan thos rang rgyal bstan/ /'khrul 'dogs las 'bras chung mi zas 'dul la/ /byang chub sems dpa' i theg pas phan 'dogs so/ /las 'bras mi rtsog rtogs pa'i blo ldan la/ /bla med rdo rje theg pa'i mthar thug go /de kun
8a4(rgyud 'grel): 'dul ba'i dbang ste bkri ba'i don/ /de dag nges par bstan la dbang ba yang/ /bde gshegs rgyal bas 'gro ba'i ched brjod pa/ /lha mi nyan thos rang rgyal theg pa la/ /mi rigs gzugs 'dzin phyi nang rten 'brel 'khor/ /mi mthun bde dang sdug bsngal
8a5(rgyud 'grel): sna tshogs kyang/ /'khrul pa de nyid snang ba ma gtogs par/ /rang bzhin dbyings las nyams pa med ces gsung/ /bden pa gnyis rtogs byang chub sems dpa' yang/ /gnyis tshul bdag dang bdag gis gzhan med de/ /rnam dag chos kyi dbyings
8a6(rgyud 'grel): las gnyis su med/ /bdag gzhan rtog pa tsam ste don du med/ /log rgyud nyid rtog rang sems skad cig ma/ /skad cig gzhi rtsa med pas chos kyi dbyings/ /bla med dngos grub gzhan nas re ba yang/ /bdag dang gzhan du rtog pa'i rgyun yin pas/ /nyid la nyid
8a7(rgyud 'grel): spyod nyid la nyid dbang bskur/ /theg pa'i khyad par rnam lngar bstan pa yong/ /'bras bu rdzogs chen theg pa cig tu gnas/ /bsod nams bsam gyis mi khyab snang ba dang/ /khyad par mngon shes drug tu snang ba yang/ /bsod nams rgyu las grub pa ma yin te/
8b1(rgyud 'grel): de nyid yang dag rtogs pa'i byin rlabs las/ /rang bzhin med las cir yang grub/ /sangs rgyas mdzad pa rims pas stod pa yang/ /'gro ba 'dul ba'i thabs las ma rtogs pa/ /sangs rgyas zhes bya mya ngan ci la 'da' / /chos kyi dbyings kyang nub bar mi 'gyur ro/ /'di
8b2(rgyud 'grel): skad bshad pa zhes kyang de phyir brjod/ /zhing khams kun tu grags pa'i snying po 'di/ /sde snod kun dang rgyud kun 'byung ba'i yum/ /de phyir snying po zhes su rgyal bas gsungs so/ /de dag bstan la 'bebs pas nges pa'ang yin/ /de phyir bstan pa yongs kyi 'byung

8b4(rgyud 'grel): dkyil 'khor kun gyi gsang ba 'di/ /sku gsung rdo rje nyid las byung/ /a ni skyed med shes rab dbyings/ /ho ni thabs mchog cho 'phrul rol/ /srid gsum 'khrul 'khor thams cad kun/ /log rtog nyid las ci yang min/ /log rtog bzhi rtsa med dbyings yin/

8b7(rgyud 'grel): 'khor lo bshad/ /gang las byung ba rnam bzhir shes bya ste/ /dgongs dang ting 'dzin ming dang 'byung khungs so/ /bde gshegs mnyam nyid dgongs pa gcig tu gyur ro/ /mnyam nyid rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor du/ /chos kun ye nas sangs rgyas ting 'dzin
9a1(rgyud 'grel): bstan/ /kun rdzob ming tsam yi ge 'phreng zhes bya/ /byung khungs ston pa'i sku gsung thugs rdo rje/ /ji ltar a byung a las ming tshogs byung/ /a dkar bzhi las a rnams phyogs bcur 'phros/ /phyogs kun gsal nas slar 'dus gzhi la thimS
9a2(rgyud 'grel): 'phros pas 'grib mang sdus pas 'phel med pa/ /spros pas gzhan don sdus pas bdag gi don/ /a 'dang ka la sogs pa bzhi bcu gnyis/ /shin tu phra ba'i tshul gyi spro bsdu pa/ /mi 'grib mi 'phel bdag gzhan don du bshad/ /a nyid rgyu ste ming tshogs
9a3(rgyud 'grel): 'bras bur gsungs/ /sku gsung thugs kyi klong nas a 'byung ste/ /a ni khongs nas 'byung bas skye ba med/ /a las 'od zer 'gur gyi gsang bar 'khyil/ /'od 'phros ka la sogs pa 'bru lngar shar/ /a'i 'od zer zla kham ljags la 'khyil

9a7(rgyud 'grel): skyes pu'i spyi gtsug 'od 'phros mgo zhes bya zer/ /'khru tshad lte ba las ni 'od 'phros shad ces bya/ /skyes bu chen po 'tshogs ma'i 'od las thig ces bya/ /gar byung bzhi bcu rtsa lnga de nyid yin/ /phyung ba'i nus mthu 'jig rten bsam? yas g.yo/ /don bshad

17a7(rgyud 'grel): rgyar snang ba yang/ /ye shes rang snang la ni ye shes rol pa bzang/ /ye shes nyid kyang sgyu ma yin phyir gsog/ rang snang bsod nams ye shes de nyid 'jig rten 'das sogs dngos grub po/ /rgyal ba gzugs sku mngon 'byung bskyob dang byin rlabs ston pa yang/ /rang sems
17b1(rgyud 'grel): rnams pa yin te gud na med/ /rang snang sgyu ma'i dkyil 'khor bya ba byed nus la/ /gzi byin rlabs 'gro la phan 'dogs pa/ /de bzhin nyid las mi gnyis 'dus ma byas pa'ang/ /mdor na rang snang sems nyid de bzhin yin phyir ro/ /sems nyid snang ba kun yang rdo rje 'dus
17b2(rgyud 'grel): ma byas ces mkhas pas bshad/ /bsgrub pa'i yan lag cho ga rnam pa lnga rdzogs par bya/ /dang po stong pa byang chub gnyis pa snying rje chen po yin/ /gsum pa yi ge bzhi pa la ni dam tshig rgya/ /lnga pa ni gzugs rdzogs gzugs ldan yin/ /yo byang gnas mchog
17b3(rgyud 'grel): yid 'od dang gdan mchog nyi zla bad sogs dang/ /phyag mtshan rdo rje dril bu'i gzungs ma mtshan ldan dang/ /a mri ta sogs phyi nang 'byor pa'i yo byad pa ldan bya/ /snying khar ye shes sems dpa' bsgom de'i snying khar nyi zla'i dkyil/ /dam tshig phyag rgya
17b4(rgyud 'grel): gzhag te de stengs yig 'bru bzhag/ zla tshes spros bsdus bzlas pa'i yan lag yin/ /bca' lnga ldan zhing dam tshig ma nyams bsgrub la brtson na 'grub/ /dus ni zla ba drug dang bcu gnyis bcu drug gis/ /tshe la dbang sogs rig 'dzin rab 'bring tha ma
17b5(rgyud 'grel): 'grub/ /'bras bu tshe dbang rigs 'dzin de nyid kyis/ /tshe lo bcu drug gis ni sku lnga lhun gyis grub/ /de ltar rig 'dzin khyad par de dag kyang/ /ye shes nyid la nyid snang bsam yas mchog/ zhing khams mi zad brgyan gyi 'khor lo ni/ /sprul pa bsam
17b6(rgyud 'grel): yas zhal mthong dang/ /mnyes nas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba yin/ /rig 'dzin rtsal gyi khyad par de nyid kyang/ /tshogs gnyis mthun te ye shes rang snang ba'o/ /gcig dang du mar bral ba'i mdza' 'das de bzhin nyid/ /rgyal bas kyang ni gzigs
17b7(rgyud 'grel): pa ma yin te/ /rab 'byung ye shes nyid la mi gnas tshul tsam snang bar zad/ /log par rtogs pas brtags pa kun kyang ye nas rnam mar cing/ /rang snang ye shes dbyings dang/ de bzhin nyid las gud na yod ma yin/ /de phyir thugs rje chen pos 'brel pa'i
18a1(rgyud 'grel): 'gro drug dus gnas mun sel snang/ /des na 'bras bu rang snang dkyil 'khor nyid du chos kun 'byung bar nges/ /don dam dkyil 'khor nyid ni stang dbyal gnyis bsam bcu/ /gsal byas dang pas zhugs nas dngos grub yid
18a2(rgyud 'grel): 'od mnyam par 'gyur/ /me tog dor te skal mnyam ye shes gang gnyer ba/ /gang gnyer ya mtshan dngos grub 'byung bar nges/ /bca' lngar mi ldan dang med dam tshig nyams na brlag par 'gyur te/ /mi 'grub gags? su 'gyur ce
18a3(rgyud 'grel): rgyal bas gsung/ /rdo rje dam tshig bkod pa'i le'u ste/ dgu pa'o// //de nas dges chen rgyal pos sbyin la snyoms zhugs te/ /dbang mchog sbyin pa 'di nyid 'gro ba'i mched du brjod/ /spyi dang khyad par ma
18a4(rgyud 'grel): thob bskyon dang rdzas dang 'bras bu lnga'o/ /spyi ni yab yum phyag rgyar bsgom te sbyor ba las/ /bde mchog yig 'bru tshogs su rdo rje'i lam nas mkha' la 'khyil/ /rdo rje rtse nas gan du stims zhing so so'i dkyil 'khor
18a5(rgyud 'grel): bsgyur/ /so so nyan dang bsgrub dang las 'chad slob dpon nyid dang lnga'o/ /nyan pa sna bar sems spros gzhal yas bdan dang bcas/ /traM gnyis las ni rin chen phyag rgya bskur gyur gsal spro thims/ /gsang gsum mnyan cha mi sma tshig
18a6(rgyud 'grel): bshad bsgrags/ /bsgrub pa snying khar de bzhin sgyu 'phrul dkyil 'khor nyid/ /rdo rje gzungs dang mchod dang sbyor dang tshig bshad bsgrags/ /las ni lag par de bzhin las rigs spro stim bya/ /lam dang pho nya byed par bka' yis rab tu bsgrags
18a7(rgyud 'grel): 'chad pa lce la pad+ma'i rigs yin te/ /snod mthun gsang ba grags pa'i tshig bshad brjod/ /slob dpon yan lag lnga la zhi khro'i tshom bu ldas/ /dkyil 'khor byed dang dang sbyin ces par bka' yis bsgrags/ /skyon ni bla ma ma mnyes lnga po ma thob par//
18b1(rgyud 'grel): lnga par rtsom pa dngos grub me brlag nges/ /de dus rdzas kyi rnam pa dgos pa yang/ /chos kyi rgyal tshab thob phyir rigs lnga'i dbu brgyan sbyin/ /shes bya ma dmongs sna tshogs dar gyi gcod pan te/ /gzugs dang ting 'dzin me tog 'phreng ba btags/ /gzhan gyis
18b2(rgyud 'grel): mi thub brgya gram go cha bskon/ /bdud las rgyal pa'i chu srin rgyal mtshan btad/ /mi d+ha mi shig rigs kyi phyag rgyas btab/ /tsha gdungs bsel phyir skyob pa gdugs kyi gdab/ /bag chags sbyangs phyin yum lnga'i bum pa bstan/ /'dod pa'i yon tan
18b3(rgyud 'grel): longs spyod bza' btung btab/ /ngos pa'i 'bras bu smin phyir snying po lnga/ /'di dag rdzas su sbyin ces rgyal bas gsung/ /'bras bu rgyal sras ngan song med pa dang/ /'jig rten tshe dang bde ba thob pa dang/ /mtho rigs lha mi thar pa'i chos kyi rgyal por 'gyur//
18b4(rgyud 'grel): dbang sbyin pa'i le'u ste/ bcu pa'o// //de nas bcom ldan 'das dgyes pa chen pos/ /rgyal po'i tshogs su dbang bskur mnyam gzhag te/ /bde ba'i mchog gi le'u 'di 'gro ba'i mched du brjod/ /rnal 'byor dgongs pa'i khyad
18b5(rgyud 'grel): par dang/ /byin rlabs bya dang sbyor sgrol dang/ /'jug pa 'bras bur bcas pa dang/ /zhi khro tshom bu'i drangs bstan pa/ /rnam pa drug gis yang dag bshad/ /dgongs pa rgyu gcig yig 'bru byin rlabs mngon sum rtogs rnams bzhi/ /rgyu gcig
18b6(rgyud 'grel): don dam kun rdzob dbyer med pa/ /ma skyes sgyu ma snang dang rang bzhin med par gcig/ a o a'oM ste sku gsung thugs rang bzhin/ /ma skyes sgyu ma dbyer med yig 'bru'i tshul/ /ras dkar dmar po tshon gyi bsgyur tshul du/ /rgyu gcig yig 'bras
18b7(rgyud 'grel): chos kun byin gyis rlobs/ /lung dang man ngag mi brten mi 'gal bar/ /rang rig blo yis mngon gsum rtogs zhes bshad/ /rtogs gzhis da chos kun mngon rdzogs rgyal po che/ /gang zhig de rtogs tshogs kyi bdag par gsung/ /rdzogs chen rdzogs
19a1(rgyud 'grel): pa'i rnal 'byor zhes kyang de la bya/ /ji ltar yan lag lnga dang dbang po lnga/ rnam shes lngas bsdus rnams smin oM du bsgoms/ /zhi khre rgyal ba yab yum byin gyis brlabs/ /'dod yon lnga sogs yul gyi rnam pa kun/ /rnam pa ma yin yi ge muM dang ?
19a2(rgyud 'grel): zhi khro dbyings phyag yum du bsgom par bya/ /gos brgyan bza' btung glu tshig bro gar sprin tshogs kun/ /byang chub sems tshogs yi ge hUM du rab bsgoms te/ /spyad dang dngos grub 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor mnyes/ /oM mu AM ? sku gsung thugs yin
19a3(rgyud 'grel): byin rlabs bya/ /sbyor ba'i gzungs ma lha klu'i bu mo 'am rigs ngan sogs/ /zhi rgyas dag la dbye ba 'am dbang drag dag la mi dbye bar/ /mnyes bsgrub rnams bzhi rim pa rab tu tsam/ /bsnyen pa don dam byang chub sems shes yin/ /nye ba'i ?
19a4(rgyud 'grel): bdag nyid phyag rgyar bsgom/ /bsgrub pa yum nyid gzungs su byin rlabs bya/ /bsgrub chen yab yum gnyis med byin rlabs la/ /mkha' las sems 'phros bdag mchod rgyal ba mnyes/ /'gro tshams
19a5(rgyud 'grel): nyi zla rdo rje lce yis dngos zos ni/ /nam mkhar 'gro dang mdog mdangs tshe ring pa/ /thun mong mchog gi bsgrub pa yin bzhin bdag por 'gyur/ /bsgral ba'i zhing 'gyur rgyu mchog rnam lnga bo/ /a 'bras rgun 'brum pa na se dang ge rgyas a ga ru//
19a6(rgyud 'grel): mchog phran gzhan yang mchog gi ga bsdus pa kun/ /blo dan 'jig rten zhes su bde gshegs gsung/ /mkhas pas a ma las ni nyi zla'i steng du bzhag/ gtsug du ye shes sems dpa' ngan song sbyongs/ /che ba'i nga rgyal bskyed cing sor mo
19a7(rgyud 'grel): 'bru bcu bsgom/ /'bru bcu'i 'od kyis rnam shes bsregs nas hUM du dag/ hUM nyid mkha' la thims par 'phangs te phyag rgyar bsgyur/ /de las sku gsal 'od 'phros brgyan dang ldan/ /gnyis su med bar bsgral zhes de la bya/ /don dam skye med
19b1(rgyud 'grel): kun rdzob mig g.yor tshul/ /sbyor sgrol byas kyang rdul tsam bya mi dmigs/ /'jug pa 'bras bcas dgra mnyam gsum rang bzhi/ /snod ni 'byung lnga gzhal yas yum du dag/ /phung po bcud rnams rgyal ba yab du dag/ tshogs brgyad sems rgyud ye shes
19b2(rgyud 'grel): lngar dag rtogs/ /de tshe don dam ma skyes dbyings su mnyam/ /kun rdzob sgyu ma phyag rgya chen por mnyam/ /shes rig lha dang yul rnams lnga mor mnyam/ /de na thams cad dkyil 'khor kun du bzang po'i zhing/ /byed spyod nyid kyang tshogs gnyis rdzogs par
19b3(rgyud 'grel): rol/ /de phyir rang bzhin lhun grub tshogs zhes gsungs/ /bkra drangs tshogs de dkyil 'khor byed ba'itshe/ /yan lag lnga bo ma nyams yo byad rnams ldar ldan/ /cho ga lnga rdzogs tshogs 'dus dkyil 'khor gyis/ /des par legs pa'i dngos grub dgongs
19b4(rgyud 'grel): ba 'grub/ /tshom bu'i grangs kyang lnga dang gsum dang gcig /rigs lnga rigs gsum rigs gcig tshom bu la/ /khro bo khro mo nyi shu'i 'khor lo bskor/ /tshom bu de kun gtso gzungs du 'khril/ /khro bo'i tshom bu grangs kyang de bzhin te/ /pho nya phyag
19b5(rgyud 'grel): brnyan bka' nyan ci bgyi rnams/ /'khor bar dngos grub las rnams rdzogs par byed/ /tshogs kyi le'u ste/ bcu gcig pa'o// //de nas rgyal po dgyes chen pos/ /rol mo sbyin 'phro brgyan bkod rnams bzhugs te/ /tshogs
19b6(rgyud 'grel): bsgrub le'u 'di 'gro ba'i mched du brjod/ /longs spyod sbyong so sor 'grub pa'i khyad par dang/ /rigs 'dzin spyi dang rigs kyi rnal 'byor dang/ /'bras bu'i khyad par gegs med khyad lnga'o/ /so so'i sgyu 'phrul bstan ba'i ting 'dzin
19b7(rgyud 'grel): gyis/ /phyag rgya lnga'i dngos grub rnam pa lnga/ /lhun gyis grub bar bde gshegs rgyal bas gsung/ /rig 'dzin shes 'jug 'bras bu khyad par bsam yas pa/ /rtogs gzhi tshul rig shes pa'i mtshan nyid yin/ /yang dang yang du gom pa
20a1(rgyud 'grel): 'jug pa ste/ /goms mthus sngon du gyur pa 'bras bu'i mtshan nyid yin/ /rgyu rkyen 'bras bu nus 'thur gang gyur pa/ /rig 'dzin zhes su rgyal ba'i zhing du grags/ /'dod khams lha mi tshangs pa'i skyes gnas su/ /skye gzhi rnams par
20a2(rgyud 'grel): dag pa 'dzin mod kyi/ /rtog pa'i khyad par sa la gnas 'gyur yin/ byang chub sa bcu bde gshegs gsum ste/ /de nyid dus ni pha rol phyin bcu byang chub pa'i rgyu/ /sbyin sogs rab dga' la sogs lhun gyis grub/ /thabs kyi kun tu 'od
20a3(rgyud 'grel): yin shes rab pad+ma can/ /thabs dang shes rab mchog 'khor lo'i tshogs chen te/ /rgyu 'bras rims don ma yin lhun gyis grub/ /khyad par sa zhes lhun grub nyid la brjod/ /rigs kyi rnal 'byor rdo rje sems dpa' nyid/ /steng
20a4(rgyud 'grel): dbyal mkha' dbyings nyi zla'i steng bsgom nas/ /rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor ma lus bsgom par 'gyur/ /de phyir rigs kyi rigs zhes brjod pa yin/ /phyogs dus kun nas sangs rgyas brtsal kyang mi rnyed te/ /rang rig sems nyid rdzogs
20a5(rgyud 'grel): sangs rgyas kyi dkyil 'khor yin/ /de phyir sems las ma rtogs sangs rgyas gzhan du ma 'tshol gcig/ rang sems rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor kun du rab sbyor bas/ /de phyir dkyil 'khor thams cad 'grub par 'gyur zhes
20a6(rgyud 'grel): rgyal bas gsung/ /rang sems dkyil 'khor nyid du rtogs chud na /cho ga lhag chas skon min gags med yin/ /de skad brjod tshes rol mos bde gshegs mnyes/ /tshogs bsgrub pa'i le'u ste/ bcu gnyis pa'o// //de nas bde
20a7(rgyud 'grel): gshegs kun kyang cig du dgongs 'dus nas/ /lhun grub dam tshig snying po'i sprin la snyoms zhugs nas/ /mdor bsdus gsang ba 'di nyid 'gro ba'i ched du brjod/ /gsang ba'i spyi dang mdo dang rgyas dang mos pa'i yon tan dang/
20b1(rgyud 'grel): rnyed dka' lam gyur rtad dang skyon dang rnam pa brgyad/ /spyi ni mi rtogs phyal ba rgyangs phan par/ /log par rtogs pa mur thugs su stegs dang/ /phyogs rgogs nyan thos rang rgyal rigs can dang/ /yang dag ma rtogs byang chub shes bya'i bsgrib/ /'dul ba'i las ni bya
20b2(rgyud 'grel): ba gnyis ga rgyud/ /dgongs ba'i don sangs phyis thub pa'i rgyud/ /rang bzhin sku gsung thugs gsang rgyud rnams kun/ /bkra shis phyir rang bzhin gsang don rbas pa rnams/ /yi ge sgra btags tshogs 'brel ming tshogs la/ /rten pa'i tshig rnams
20b3(rgyud 'grel): kyis ni rab mtshon ste/ /dgongs pa'i dbang gis don gnyis bag cing sbas/ /kun gyi khongs na gnas pa'i don de gsang ba 'di las 'byin mdzad pa'i/ /theg pa kun la mkhas pa ston pa'i thugs la gnas/ /de phyir gsang ba'i snying po de
20b4(rgyud 'grel): kho na/ /de nyid nges pa'i khongs nas phyung zhes ston pas gsungs/ /'byung gnas bstan la phebs ces de nyid yin/ /sna tshogs don 'chad smra zhing ston ces de la bya/ /mdo don dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis bsdus bshad pa/ /dkyil 'khor
20b5(rgyud 'grel): de bzhin nyid ces bya bar bshad/ /de bzhin nyid ldan rang bzhin dkyil 'khor gyis/ /gzugs brnyan lhag pa'i gzugs brnyan dkyil 'khor la/ /ting 'dzin lhag ba'i ting 'dzin dkyil 'khor bsgom/ /tshogs chen bya ba dkyil 'khor
20b6(rgyud 'grel): nyid yin te/ /dkyil 'khor las byung thugs rjes 'dul bar bshad/ /thugs ni byang chub rnams gnyis dkyil 'khor yin/ /lhun gyis grub pa'i dkyil 'khor mchog du gsung/ /bcu gnyis nyid du rgyud kyi don rdzogs te/ /gsang ba'i
20b7(rgyud 'grel): man ngag ces kyang de phyir brjod/ /rgyas pa de bzhin nyid ni rtogs dka' gsang ba spros med thig le te/ /dkyil 'khor kun 'byung phyir ni dbyings ces gsungs/ /rang bzhin 'byung lnga dngos med shes rab yum/ /chen po rags
21a1(rgyud 'grel): pa thabs te yab lnga yin/ /gnyis med sems las sprul pa'i lha tshogs ni/ /dbang drug yul drug dus bzhi rnam pa drug/ phyin phyi ma log rang bzhin dkyil 'khor yin/ /rang bzhin kun tu bzang po'i dkyil 'khor
21a2(rgyud 'grel): la/ /thugs kyi ye shes lnga nyid byang chub sems yin te/ /rnal 'byor bdag nyid chen po'i byang chub sems/ /snying po'i thig ler chos kun mnyam sbyar lhag par bshad/ /rnal 'byor ba de ba'i tshogs mchog mi zad rol mo
21a3(rgyud 'grel): kyis/ /ye shes dges pa'i lha la mchod 'bul tshogs zhes bya/ /zag med rang rig bsod nams rgyu nyid kyis/ /yi shes rang snang sgyu ma'i dkyil 'khor rol mo mdza' yas mchog/ de nyid ting nge 'dzin te lhag pa'i ting 'dzin 'dam?
21a4(rgyud 'grel): pa'i thig le yum gyi dbyings/ /thig le de nyid sangs rgyas kun gyi dngos gzhi yin/ /bde gshegs sku sogs bdag gi zhal mthong ba/ /rig pas dbang bsgyur dngos grub dam pa gzugs brnyan rnams gnyis yin/ /lhun

21a6(rgyud 'grel): sbyar las/ /snying rje chen po'i dkyil 'khor mi zad yongs kyi 'byung/ /phyogs dus 'gro ba'i dkyil 'khor sprul pas 'dul ba yis/ /mgon po ji snyed sgyu ma'i dkyil 'khor thabs kyis sgrol ba yang/ /bya byed med par spyod pas
21a7(rgyud 'grel): 'dul ba'i dkyil 'khor yin par bde gshegs gsungs/ /mos pa'i yon tan bcu gnyis shes rab gsum gyis mnyam sbyar bas/ /rang 'byung dkyil 'khor stod dam lhun gyis grub/ /'di las rgyal ba mchog kyang d+ha bar
21b1(rgyud 'grel): gal mdzad/ /gang zhig dkyil 'khor 'di dag kun la mos pa'i skyes bu la/ /phyogs dus rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor ma lus kun/ /sras kyi dam pa mchog du dgongs par 'gyur/ /'di ni rnyed dka' bskal pa rdul rnyed sbyangs pas snyen pa'o/ /'bras
21b2(rgyud 'grel): bu gsang chen nges pa 'di yin te/ /drug gi 'jig rten phyogs bcu 'das dang da ltar rgyal ba yang/ /gsang ba 'di snyed sku lnga lhun gyis grub pa yin/ /de bzhin 'byung dang ma 'ongs 'od yis grub/ /de'i phyir 'di ni gsang tshan nges pa'i 'bras bu
21b3(rgyud 'grel): lam gyur yin/ /rgyal ba sras bcas kun la'ang 'di las des don gzhan mi mnga' / /gzhan nas rtsal bas rgyal bas kyang ni rnyed par ga la 'gyur/ /'ji gtad rgyud kun las ni 'byung ba'i phyag rgya'i mchog/ shes rab gsum gyis sbyangs pa'i
21b4(rgyud 'grel): dmigs ldan rnams kyis gzung/ /snod ldan dang tshul bzang la blo brtan pa/ /lus dang longs spyod stong phod tsam las ma rtogs gzhan du mi sbyin no/ /gal te sbyin na rmongs 'phyar de nyid srog zang ngan 'gror ltung/ /shin tu gsang ba man ngag snying
21b5(rgyud 'grel): po'i le'u ste/ bcu gsum pa'o// //de nas dges pa chen po'i glu 'di blangs/ /glu drug blangs pas sangs rgyas che ba'i yon tan kun rdzogs phyir/ /dang po tshogs chen gnyis su brtan pa dang/ /gnyis pa rdo rje rnam bzhir brjod pa
21b6(rgyud 'grel): yin/ /gsum pa rdzogs chen rnam pa bzhir grags so/ /bzhi pa las ni mdza' yas bzhi zhes bshad/ /lnga pa rdul snyed rnam pa bzhir stong pa/ /drug pa sku gsung thugs ni rnam pa bzhi/ /nyi shu rtsa bzhi bstong pa'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs/ /mnyes
21b7(rgyud 'grel): pa'i le'u ste/ bcu bzhi pa'o// //de nas bde gshegs rgyal po'i rgyal ba bdag po des/ /khro bo'i dkyil 'khor nyid du mngon par 'du mdzad de/ /ci'i phyir ji ltar ltul nas las bskos mdzad dang gsum/ /ci phyir 'dul
22a1(rgyud 'grel): mdzad rnam pa gsum yin te/ /khams gsum pa'i rgyu dang rkyen dang 'bras bu'o/ /rgyu ni bdag rtogs la sogs dmongs pa'i bar/ /srid pa'i sa bon rtsub mos 'phangs pa rkyen yin te/ /'bras bu dmyal ba yi dags srin po
22a2(rgyud 'grel): gsum/ /ru tra rnams gsum zhes kyang de la bya/ /ji ltar 'dul dbang dag gis drug 'dul te/ /che mchog nyid dang khro bo mchol pa dang/ /rdo rje zhe sdang dang ni rdo rje srin po dang/ /rdo rje khro bo dang ni 'jigs byed khro bo'o/ /cha mchog khro bo'i ting nge 'dzin
22a3(rgyud 'grel): snyoms zhugs nas/ /gnyis med mdza' las khro bo 'chol pa bstan no/ /de ni tshe mchog dkyil 'khor dang po yin/ /khro bo 'chol pas rdul snyed cho 'phrul ston/ /phyogs bcu'i de pa thams cad 'dul bar mdzad/ /dkyil 'khor gnyis pa zhes ni da la bya/ /de nas
22a4(rgyud 'grel): che mchog dbus kyi rtsor bsgyur te/ /phyogs bcu'i khro bo 'dus nas rigs bzhir gyur/ /gzung bcas gregs pa gnon pa'i 'phrin las mdzad/ /zhe sdang rdo rje zhes bya'i dkyil 'khor gsum pa'o/ /dreg pa nga rgyal ston pa 'dul ba'i phyir/ de nyid dbu dgu srin
22a5(rgyud 'grel): par snang bar 'gyur/ /rdo rje srin po bsgral nas zhal du stob/ /dbang phyug ma rnams sngags kyi bsdu ba mdzad/ /de ni srin po'i dkyil 'khor bzhi pa'o/ /de nyid khrag 'thung rigs ldan snang byas te/ /dbang phyug ma rnams so so'i sku la 'khril/ /re re las kyang phra men nyi shu'i

27a5(rgyud 'grel): nges don la/ /rnam gsum tshul gyis phyag 'tshal lo/ /gzhi rang bzhin rkyen kyis spyan mdongs pas/ /shes bya gnyi rgyud sa la rmongs pa dag/ gzhi mthong nas thob phyi yi ge rgyud/ /spyan gyi /mkha' rtsa drang mchog gssum ga sngags skyen sal dang
27a6(rgyud 'grel): bye/ /dod dam kun rdzob dbyer med de la nges pa'i don gyi rgyud/ chi ba dam bca' ba bston/ 'khrul? pa'i thun mong thams cad rang rig ma yi bzhi lam na pa'i lung/ ma bslang nam mkha' 'dra par 'bras bu /dngos ston rgyur? thams? cad kyi rgyan? po pa'i mchog/ /? gzhi lam thi 'bras lung? kyi 'grel pa/ kun las
27a7(rgyud 'grel): spyi don zhi pa la dri ste che ba dang mdor bstan pa dang rgyas pa'o/ /? pa thugs rgyal? dang po che ba bstan nyi ma 'dra ba'i gyi mi sde snod kun dang chung rgyal ba'i dal ma lus pa theg pa bzhi yis /'bras mthar thug ba'i 'dren pa rnam pa ? lam
27b1(rgyud 'grel): don/ /ri? rgyal bla na med pa kun gyi yum du mkha' las 'byung lnga gyur pa/ /tshig dkrugs pa bstebs te /don bshad pa'i rgyud 'di'i spyan rnam par dbye ba yang rnam pa gsum ste/ gang zhe na/ chos nyid rang bzhin gyi rnal 'byor phyi mo'i rigs mi 'gyur
27b2(rgyud 'grel): ? ba thams cad rdo rjes ma theg pa'i rtsa chad 'bul ba ste drang pa nyid dang/ gnyis pa mdor bstan pa la gnyis kyi dang po rigs pas mdor bstan pa mngon du byed pa'i rnal 'byor rgyud du 'byung zhing mi gtong bar byed pa rtsol ba'i rigs dang/ mthar thug gi rnal 'byor pa ba med pa'i
27b3(rgyud 'grel): rgyud du byung zin pas mi 'gyur pa 'bas? du'i rigs so/ /de yang bye brag bstan pa las/ gtan tshigs tshad ma gsum gyi dngos po yi/ /rnal 'byor gsum gyi phung po la/ /rigs dang snang ba'i yan lag gzhag /de nyid thur? ma'i mchog tu nges//
27b4(rgyud 'grel): ces gsungs so/ /de la ce bral bstan pa man ngag gi rjes su gnyis pa lung gi bstan pa'o 'grel pa'i lugs nyid ni 'di lung man yig pa lta ste/ thog mar phyi gzhal yas mo'i rnal 'byor ni/ bsgrub rta ? gas pa'i yul spros pan dang tshangs dri bral ba las khyad ?
27b5(rgyud 'grel): rgyab ? dring dang be rang bzhin snang ba bzhi'i dang po phyi mo'i bdug tshul pa gnyis kyi dang po ngo bo du ngo bos gyur pa chos nyid kyi rigs ste/ bstsal bya ril gyi dngos gzhi 'phel 'grib dang bral ba kho na ste/ bzhi/ de la ni ma bslang ma brtags ji bzhin pa'i phyir/ bye bra dbus? ? mi ?
27b6(rgyud 'grel): pas dang po'i ming nges par 'thob bo/ /de lung gis brtan par gnyid pa nges tshig bya gzhung nyid las/ de la chos nyid kyi rigs lam ni kun la khyab par yod do/ /zhes gsungs pa dang/ tha snyad du ma bcos nam mkha' i dbyings ni bsam yas
27b7(rgyud 'grel): par ces pa'i ? la mtshan zlog gung ces pa tshi spyi do/ gnyis pa lung gas bshad brgyad gsungs so/ rgyas pa nas /de la spyi don gsum la gnyis kyi ngo bo dang ni tha snyad du rang bzhin gyi snang ba zhes kyang bsnyad de ? /'on kyang rang bzhin snang ba'i snang chu ston/ rgyas pa nas phan tshun las grol bar
28a1(rgyud 'grel): 'chad pas/ yul can du mi 'gyur te/ dper na rgya mtsho nyid rlabs lta bu'o/ /de yang shes rab dang gtan tshigs kyis byas pa ma yin pa'i phyir/ nges tshig 'grub pa'o/ /'di nyid kyang gnyis kyang? tho dang rgyas pa'o rnam pa med pa'i rnam pa
28a2(rgyud 'grel): gnyis su 'gyur te/ ji ba yul dang zhin pa rang bzhin gyi de kho na nyid dang/ mun gnyis pa rang bzhin snang ba 'dis tshig go pa'i rang bzhin glo bur du snang pa'o/ /'o na de rgya cis snyam pa la/ dang po spyi don gsum pa la la rnam pa med kyang gnyis pa la gnas pas/ mthong ba nges par
28a3(rgyud 'grel): spyir? na bzhi pa la gnyis te mdor bstan dang rgyas pa'o/ /ma byas pas/ /rnam pa med pa la yod par mthong ba ni/ me long ? can lta bu ste/ 'di nyid las/ me long g.yas rgyas pa la ? gyi dang po 'khrul snang ba gnyis kyi dngos po ma nges pas 'byung bar yog pa dang 'dra ste/ gzugs brnyan snang ba'i bya ba byed shes par
28a4(rgyud 'grel): mi nus so/ /zhes gsungs so/ /'di nyid kyi don nges par rang cha rnam grangs chud par bya ba'ang/ rgyal po drag shul can gyis zhus pa las /gser la gzo'i rnam pa ltar/ /snang ba dang po rang rig pa/ /yul med gnyis phyir mthong med phyir/ /brtags pas tha dad gyur pa ste/
28a5(rgyud 'grel): de yang 'byung tshul bzhi ba/? gnyis la rang gis ma nas bzhed gnyis khongs su 'gyur/ /des na ma nges chad pa'i rigs/ /rang gi ngo'i sgyu? 'phrul pos dang po nyid/ /skabs ming gnyis su gyur pas phye/ /zhes gsu ? gzung 'dzin ngas pa ni/ /ji ltar zhe na/ dper gser la 'du byed kyis
28a6(rgyud 'grel): tha dad pa mchog gnas dang/ rgyan gyi rnam pa dang/ brgyad du snod ji ltar snang la ngo bo gcig pas/ nye bar mtshon pa ni/ ji bzhin pa'i dag pa rnal ? kyang ? rang bzhin dad 'khrul snang byor te de yang ngo bo dang mtshan nyid ril lhun gyis grub pa'i bdag nyid ni/ mdza' kun
28a7(rgyud 'grel): bral nyag cig ci yang ma spangs pa/ phyogs med phyogs kyi dngos gzhi pa/ ris can ris dang bral ba ni/ sgron ma sprul pa nyid kyis kyang 'di zhes brtag par mi zin pa ni/ sgro skur dang ngang gis bral bas skabs las nges pa'i lung zhes kyang bsnyad?
28b1(rgyud 'grel): de/ 'di nyid las/ thams cad rang rig byang chub sems/ /de ni lung gi tshad mar bshad/ /tshang bzhi phab pa'i don yin te/ zhe'/ /'o na mun pa'i snang ba byung ba rigs gnyis kyi dngos po 'di dag 'byung bar mi rigs so snyam pa la/ de ni rang gi byung tshul brgyad kyi
28b2(rgyud 'grel): 'grel te/ rgyu rkyen 'bras bu 'byung pa'i dus/ /tshul dang nyes pa 'grub byed pa/ /nye bar mtshon pas rnam par dbye/ /zhor la spyi'i 'khrul snang gi gnyis pa la gnyis kyi dris pa dgos bshad rgyu rkyen pa'o/ /ces 'byung pas/ rigs kun la 'jug pa dang lan la gnyis kyi mdor bstan/ chang pa'i 'og
28b3(rgyud 'grel): ba grong khyer gsum du 'khor ba dag gi rgyu ni/ /rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ ma rig rtog pa'i gzung 'dzin gyis/ zhes pa dang/ kun gzhi snang pa nyid bral te /rtag tu brgyad ? bshad pa rang mtshan gsal la rgyas pa la dgu'i dang po gyur chos nyid kyang/ /zhen pas snang ba rigs ra ma gyur
28b4(rgyud 'grel): na/ /mig snang ba mi snang phyed snang gis mig bzhin ma rig pa'o/ /zhes gsungs ste/ mi rig pa dang/ bag chags dang/ las? sgyu 'phrul rgya mtsho las/ dang dang ma shes /nyon mongs pa ni/ mthong 'di lhan cig byed pa dang/ nye bar len pa dang/ mtshung gzung 'dzin sa par don ldan pa'i las
28b5(rgyud 'grel): bya'i ? phye bas rgyu kho na'o/ /'khor ba'i rigs gnyis kyi rkyen ni/ bsod nams dang/ bsod nams ma yin pa dag mi g.yo ba'i las dang/ nyon mongs pa brtags pa lnga 'phra rags dang mang nyung gis so sor sbyar ba'o/ de yang dge bcu spyod cing mi dge slong?
28b6(rgyud 'grel): byed pa/ zhes pa dang/ tha ma gnyis pa skyabs can gzung 'din? mnyam par ma shes na/ /ma lus kun la zhe sdang cing/ /zhes pa rnams dang/ yang chod med bzhi spyod mig khams dri med kun yong yo sgom byed pa/ zhes pa la sogs pa rgyas dge bcu par bstan to/ /smin pa
28b7(rgyud 'grel): ni/ rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ sna tshogs lus dang longs spyod dang/ zhes ? rgyu pa dag gis ston to/ bzhi pa dus /snang pa'i dus ni/ thog ma med mi g.yo ba'i las nas sems yan btang/ zhes pas ston te/ ltos pa'i glo bur ba yin no/ sdug bsngal /gsum pa 'bras? 
29a1(rgyud 'grel): de'i tshe 'khor brten cing 'brel pa'i grangs dang phra rags kyi chas gnas so sor 'khor ba ste/ rtsa ba las/ phyi nang rten 'brel gnyis su 'khor/ ces gsungs so/ /tshul des na yang dag pa'i lam dang phral zhing
29a2(rgyud 'grel): sna tshogs kyi gtse lnga pa tshul ba myong ba'o/ /de yang mi mthun rten 'brel khams cha 'phrad? yod pas bde sdug myong bar 'gyur/ snying po zhes pa dang/ ye shes lnga'i don ma rtogs pa/ zhes pas gas drug pa nyes pa la lo/ /de grub par byed pa'o ni/
29a3(rgyud 'grel): skad ma cig ma gnyis kyis snang ba'i phyogs gcig ste/ ma bcos rgyun gyi skad cig ma/ /de yis ma byas gang yang med/ /ces gsungs so/ /de dag nye bar mtshon pa ni/ rtsa? dang sog me 'khor lo bzhi bdun pa byed pa po na/ /long btags rgyas?
29a4(rgyud 'grel): shing brgyud par rang bzhin dang rgyun gyi 'gyur/ zhes rgyud kyi skad cig gsungs/ /de ji ltar snang yang rang gi ngo bo rtag pa gnyis dang bral ba thog ma'i rnal brgyad pa dpe 'byor nyid do/ /de yang/ sbyir ni log rtog bsam yas pa/ /ye nas yo rtog pa nga pa ma yin
29a5(rgyud 'grel): te/ /chi yang med las cing yang snang/ /snang ba nyid na ngo bo med/ dbu ? zhar la bshad pa la dril dang po gnyis med du ces ? thug rgyun pas bya ba rdzogs pa dang dus kyi mthas gsungs so/ /de dag bkod pa ni ngo bo nyid de lta bas na/ dngos po brgyad so so nas rang bzhin gyis
29a6(rgyud 'grel): sangs rgyas pas/ cig dang du ma las grol ba'i rigs rtogs par bya ba'i chad do/ /de bas ming ? 'dzin gis phye yang ngo bo la tha dad med pa'i phyir/ gnyis pa brkyang ngo'i dgos ched dang ye snang stong gnyis med pa nas rgyu rkyen sogs pa ngo bo yong yin na/ /

29b1(rgyud 'grel): song 'gro drug sna tshogs rgyu ba yang/ /'khrul ba'i blo log rtog pa nyid snang ste/ /de bzhin nyid la gyur cing nyams pa med/ ces pas snang ba'ang 'gyur ro// spyi don gnyis pa // de la grub ba'i rnal 'byor mthar thug

29b4(rgyud 'grel): gnyis kyis rang gi rang bzhin mngon du byas pas tha mal pa dang/ bcud gcig pa'i zhen pa man chad spangs pa'i ye shes ni/ ril lhun kyis grub pas/ skyed du bya ba med pa dang/ spyod spyi don gnyis pa la lnga'i dang po dam tshig
29b5(rgyud 'grel): yul bral bas ming rnal nges par 'grub pa skye ba'o/ /de ltar kun 'od 'thob pa'i skabs kyang 'bras bu ril bdag nyid pa'i phyir/ thob bya gzhan du rag ma lus 'bras bu pa'i phyir na/ tha mal pa'i dbang du yang lhag

29b7(rgyud 'grel): tan la lnga ste /lam du gyur te 'bras du sku dang /lnga'i gsum pa ngo bo gsung dang/ thugs dang/ yon tan dang/ 'phrin la bla med rigs sa ste/ re re la yang lnga lngar bye brag lnga lngar gyur pa'o/ lnga'i bzhi ba /de dag gi mtshan nyid ni
30a1(rgyud 'grel): gcig dang du ma'i cha rnams ma pa snyigs bral bas gzung dka' ba'o/ /de dag nye bar mtshon ba ni/ nor bu rin po che dang/ gar mkhan dang/ brag cha dang/ nyi ma rgya mtsho

30b1(rgyud 'grel): zhes gsungs pa dang/ thabs kyi zhags pa las kyang/ rgyal ba'i rgyal ba rnams kyi sku/ /rna tshogs cing yang snang mod kyang/ /kun tu rin chen lta bu ste/ zhes pa dang/ rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ dper na gar mkhan nyid 'dra ba/ /lus las ma
30b2(rgyud 'grel): god sna tshogs ston/ /dpar na brag cha'i sgra bzhin no/ /ston nyid sgyu ma mig yor tshul/ /ces pa la sogs yon tan pa gsungs so/ /de bas na 'di nyid 'phrin las las mthon dmankun gyi
30b3(rgyud 'grel): gzugs snang dang/ bla med byang chub gsung skur snang ba/ /sku me long lta bu tshul bzhin du/ /sna tshogs kha dog dbyibs su snang/ ces bzhi ba 'dug bsdus te bstan pa'o gsungs pas/ de la ni bde par

30b6(rgyud 'grel): ni gzhi dang dang skyes nges pa/ gnyis su/ gzhi rig rgyu can dang gcig sems bskyed nas mi ldog pa'i dang lam rigs bzhi/ /gsang la chen rgyas pa la gnyis kyi dang por pa'i dbye ba dang bla med g.yo ldang gnas smon 'jug mthar phyin mi ldog 'dod / zhes

31a1(rgyud 'grel): yan pa'i/ /dbye bas gnyis 'gyur ma yin pa'ang/ /shes pa lnga'i yul min pa'i/ /dam pa'i shes pa gnyis pa'i/ /yul 'gyur ngo bo rgyu 'bras kyis/ /lung gi spyir ru grags pa nyid/ /
31a2(rgyud 'grel): rnam par bshad pas lnga ru la 'gyur ro/ sngags byen/ su zhes cu nor ga nang la sungs mun pa pa log sred pa'i byis pas phyogs dam pa'i pa'i phyir/ gsang sngags /bka' i nang pa'i spyod pa/ de nyid khu kun gyi spyi ru 'di dbu zhabs su don lnga ste/ gang zhe

31b5(rgyud 'grel): 'khor gyi nang nas skal mchog nang tshad ldan tshad/ rgya ? pa'i tshad /'dul ba'i dus bzhugs tshul/ nang tshul du thig le thig bran du bab phyi tshul du ston 'khor du gsang pa'i bdag /
31b6(rgyud 'grel): bzhi pa bsdud? ba shes rang? mchog gi ma bsdus la bde ba gshegs mi gnas mnyam nyid dang du byon/ /lag na rdo rjes bsdu pa mdzad/ lnga ba dus/ de tshe dus nyid mdza' bral phyir/ /ngo po dus bzhi
32a1(rgyud 'grel): mnyam pa nyid/ /rgyal ba sems dpa' rnal 'byor pa/ /dgongs pa rig pa rna bas brgyud/ /gsang ba'i snying po de kho na/ /nyid de nges pa'i dbyings nas phyung/ /zhes gsungs pa dag ni gzhi ste/
32a2(rgyud 'grel): skabs 'dir rtsa ba'i rgyud las drug pa bstan pa bdud rtsi ro yis sga ba bde chen 'brub ces pa/ gsungs pa dang/ de nyid dkrugs pa gang brgyud na/ rgyud kyi phyir klad du ma bkod de/ rkyen yang rjes su mthun par sbyar ro/ /'di dag gdul bya'i skabs
32a3(rgyud 'grel): dkyus kyi nges bzung ni rtsa ba'i rgyud ltar ro/ kyis snang ba gzhan dag kyang gnyis te/ sgyu 'phrul gyi rgyud las/ 'di zhes nye bar mtshon pa ni/ /e sogs rnam bzhi dbyibs can rtsa rgyud las gnas/ /skad ni gnyis pa thun mong ma yin bla? gnyis kyi dang po gsang bar
32a4(rgyud 'grel): gsal byed las ming can/ /bi dbyibs thig ler bcas ston pa'o/ /me ta ma nu sdom byed yid/ /'khor las chen rnam shes de dag la/ /gsal bar snang ba bshad sdud 'dod/ /pa sgra don dam nges pa'i rgyud/ /yan theg chen 'di yin no/ /dus

42a1(rgyud 'grel): phan? tshun 'gyed ba'i thabs nyid ni/ /sems mdza' 'od bas go phye nas/ rang snang thabs kyis gnas sbyar ba'i/ /zung 'jug thabs chen de las byung/ gnyis med ye shes rdo rje che/ /rgyu rkyen gzhan las byung ba min/ zhes
42a2(rgyud 'grel): gsungs so/ /'o na 'bras snang ba rnam 'byed ces phyag rgya spros pa/ bu de lam gyis bstsal bas gzod 'byung bar chad med pa tshogs/ ngo zhe na/ ji snyed tshe dbang brjod pa'i kha brgyud kyang/ /'bras bu yang dag don gyi snying po ni/ /gang nas btsal kyang mi snyed

42b1(rgyud 'grel): a 'is bod de rab tu bsdus/ ces gsungs so/ /byang chub pa'i mtshan nyid gang snyam pa la/ de bzhin nyid kyi ye shes ni/ /gcig ces 'di zhes brjod du med/ /gnyis med dbyings kyi dang du med/ /gsum du sna tshogs 'byung
42b2(rgyud 'grel): zhing 'phro/ zhes pa de ltar lhun gyis grub pa'i don ma lta ba bstan lnga bslad ma bcos pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i rgyu'i pa tan tshigs suAng mtshan nyid ni/ mdza' rnams ma spangs bral la ma bsdus rdzogs pa'i sems nyid bye brag gi chos su

42b4(rgyud 'grel): 'o na yon tan ci 'ang mi snang ba zhig go zhe na/ mdza' 'i sgros pa rang bral ba'i sems nyid 'di sku gsung thugs mi zad pa rgyan kyi 'khor lor rang snang ba'i tshang rtog ge'i blos dpag ba las 'das pa'i phyir/ byin mnyam pa'i dbyings

42b6(rgyud 'grel): gyi phyag rgya bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor du sangs rgyas pa ni bsgrub bya dang shes bya dam pa kho na nges pa'i lung rang bzhin gyi rgyud do/ /de las gzhan pags bar smra bas 'di mi thong pa'i phyir/ /de las lhag pa'i don
42b7(rgyud 'grel): smra ba/ /de ni rnam dgra lam yin te/ /rang blo bsam pas 'khrul pa yin zhes pa/ /sgyu 'phrul rgya mtsho bshad rgyud las/ /phyogs du sa rgyal ba'i ngo bo nyid/ /mi srid? 'khor lo rang snang don/ /mi mthong rmongs pa'i 'khrul pa
43a1(rgyud 'grel): rnams/ /byin rlabs lha dang yon tan lhar/ snang 'dod res 'jog sems 'dod sogs/ /gzhan las 'phags 'dod nor pa'i lam/ /mdongs pas nam mkha' brnyebs pa bzhin/ nor bsam nor rnyed mi
43a2(rgyud 'grel): 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de'i 'bras bu'i ngo bo nyid gang snyam pa la/ thams cad rang rig byang chub sems/ de ni lung gi tshad mar bshad/ /tshang bzhi phab pa'i don yin te/ zhes pa snang ba dang/ zhen pa bzhis bsdus
43a3(rgyud 'grel): pa ril rang gi mtshan nyid rig pa dang gsal ba de nyid mdza' ma spangs bral ba la ril lhun kyis grub par gsal ba la mi g.yo ba'i don ni sgro skur dang dang gis bral bar bden pa lam pa'i snang ba 'khrul snang rang bzhin gyis
43a4(rgyud 'grel): kho zhe na kha gcig ched du byas pa'i zhen pa/ na'o/ /de ni dbral du gtan tshigs kyis bsgrub par bya ba dang bral te/ phyi mo nas lung dang rigs pa dang mngon gsum dang rjes dpag thun mong ma yin pa dag gi grub mdza' grub zin
43a5(rgyud 'grel): pas ma nor ma bslad pa'i shes bya'o/ /lhag min skabs kyis bsgom lam dag dang 'brel par 'chad pa'o/ /bsgom lam gang zhe na/ dag pa rnam gsum tshul sgom zhing/ zhes pa/ snod bcud rgyud dag par
43a6(rgyud 'grel): bshad pa'i don gsum gyis rtogs par bya ba'i don du na lta ba yang dbye thag bcad de/ de nyid ji lta bar rig pa rang gsal la mi g.yo bar bya ba'o/ /byed par 'brel pa'i sgra ni/ dper nyi mas 'od mi 'tshol ba ltar tha snyad du mnyam
43a7(rgyud 'grel): par 'jog par rtag ? lta bas/ stsom? pa skad zer yang dngos po bdag nyid pas dang po dang dre? bzhis drang blo rjes su 'brengs pa med pa'i phyir// zhing bya ba dang po ltar byas pa med med la spyod btung bya med bya/ zhes gsungs so//

43b2(rgyud 'grel): dang rang bzhin gsung du/ 'bras bu bstan lnga'i bdag nyid du yod pa'i phyir ro/ /gzhan du na sgyu 'phrul rgya mtsho las/ /rtsa bcud shes pa'i ngo bo nyid/ /thabs kyis yab yum ye shes gsol/ /de nyid rten can rten lnga lngar/ /rang gnas thabs
43b3(rgyud 'grel): kyi bdag nyid du/ /nyon mongs sa bon kun kyang gnas/ /de phyir gzhan bshad rgyud la rag ma lus/ /ces dag pa rnam gsum gsungs so/ /rnal 'byor dang po'i don to/ /de nyid dang longs bde stong spyod 'bu lngar? du bstan pa gang snyam pa la/ zang pa'i
43b4(rgyud 'grel): dus med yid bzhin mdzod/ /bum pa bzang dang ye shes su yid bzhin mdzod/ /za ma tog dang rin chen rkyal/ /gzhan nas yod 'ongs ma yin te/ /rang sems bsod nam 'bras bu bstan sa brtan bdag pa yin zhes pa/ /mi zad rgyan kyi 'khor lo'i//

44a1(rgyud 'grel): bo'o/ /de rngos gang zhe na/ bo de dkor ni rin po chen/ /sku gsung mi bzang bar ldan pa'i/ /rgyan gyi dkyil 'khor bsam mi khyab zhes pa/ /byang chub kyi dkor ni bdun kho nar 'dus par 'chad par 'gyur te/ dpe'i ni dgos 'dod
44a2(rgyud 'grel): skong ba dang 'phel 'grib med pa dang/ rtog pa bral ba'i chos bzhis sbyar to/ /de'i mtshan nyid dang ched ni gcig du ma las grol bas gcig la 'ang ril lhun gyis rdzogs pa'i po de dkor na rin po che/ dkyil 'khor smra brjod bsam pa las 'das pas

57b2(rgyud 'grel): rgyud kyi rgyu dang dkyil 'khor chog nyid dang chad pa thun mong du bstan pa'i phyir/ le'u lnga'i spyan rnam par dbye ba la brtsams par 'jug par bya'o/ /de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid la zhugs nas/ zhes pa/ ston pa dang 'khor
